Destiny is Calling Me

"+ "

The President hadn't felt this free in decades. The staffers had abandoned the castle; his wife was home; the Secret Service agents were drinking. The perfect night to get away from it all. On November 4th, 2008, Al Gore would let loose.

"+ "

His legacy was cemented, and Romney would be President. He would wipe the slate clean, erase his work, and the people would miss him. They'd want him back. That would be enough.

"+ "
